''''' PrÃžfung Benutzernamen '''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''
'
'Diese Abfrage PrÃžft den Benutzernamen von Excel
'Folgende Benutzer mÃžssen vor dem schlieÃen die Bewertung "TEA, TEK,KMU" vornehmen.
'Ist der Benutzer in der Vorhandern wird in Zelle A10 eine "1" geschrieben.
'Ist der Benutzer nicht Vorhandern wird in Zelle A10 eine "" geschrieben.
'
'
Select Case (VBA.Environ("Username"))
Case "petersmeier"
    bAktion = True
Case "kuhlenkord"
    bAktion = True
Case "rinsche"
    bAktion = True
Case "brakweh"
    bAktion = True
Case "uceda"
    bAktion = True
Case "kschlueter"
    bAktion = True
Case "elkenkamp"
    bAktion = True
Case "mielchen"
    bAktion = True
Case Else
    bAktion = False
End Select

If bAktion = True Then
ActiveSheet.Range("A10").Value = 1
End If

If bAktion = False Then
ActiveSheet.Range("A10").Value = ""
'Call starten
End If

'End If
'End If

ActiveSheet.Columns(25).Hidden = True
Else

Private Sub Worksheet_Change(ByVal Target As Range)

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False


    Dim rng As Range, colZ As New Collection, ii As Long

    Dim rngstart1 As Integer
    Dim rngende1 As Integer
    Dim rngstart2 As Integer
    Dim rngende2 As Integer
    
    Dim rngBereich As Range
    Dim c As Range
    Dim ZeileStart As Integer
    Dim ZeileEnde As Integer
    
    rngstart1 = Range("A3").Value + 1
    rngende1 = Range("A4").Value - 1
    rngstart2 = Range("A5").Value + 1
    rngende2 = Range("A6").Value - 1
    
    
If Not Intersect(Target, Range("Bereich_Gesamt")) Is Nothing Then ActiveSheet.Range("A2").Value = 1
    
''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''
''' Hier wird der wirksame Bereich fÃžr die automatische ZeilenhÃķhenanpassung festgelegt.
For Each rng In Target           ' falls mehrere Zellen auf einmal geÃĪndert
    If (rng.Row >= 21 And rng.Row <= 27) Or _
         (rng.Row >= 37 And rng.Row <= 43) Or _
         (rng.Row >= rngstart1 And rng.Row <= rngende1) Or _
         (rng.Row >= rngstart2 And rng.Row <= rngende2) Then       'Ãžberwachte Zeilennummern - anpassen
         On Error Resume Next
         colZ.Add rng.Row, CStr(rng.Row)     ' hier werden Dubletten vermieden
         On Error GoTo 0
   End If
   Next rng
   For ii = 1 To colZ.Count
      ZeilenhoeheVerbundene colZ(ii) ' HÃķhen der gesammelten Zeilen optimieren (Modul 1)
   Next ii
   Set colZ = New Collection
   
'''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''
''' Wird der Inhalt einer Zeile im Bereich Technische Ãnderungen gelÃķscht so wird das "X" auch gelÃķscht

On Error Resume Next
   ZeileStart = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A5").Value + 1
   ZeileEnde = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1

Set rngBereich = Range(Cells(ZeileStart, 3), Cells(ZeileEnde, 3))  ' Bereich der Wirksamkeit

If Not Intersect(Range(Target.Address), rngBereich) Is Nothing Then
            If Target.Value = "" Then
            ActiveCell.Offset(0, 1).Value = ""
            ActiveCell.Offset(0, 4).Value = ""
            ActiveCell.Offset(0, 5).Value = ""
End If
End If

'''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''
''' Wird im Bereich Technische Ãnderungen der Inhalt geÃĪndert oder gelÃķscht dann wird die Schriftfarbe wieder auf Blau gesetzt.
On Error Resume Next
   
   ZeileStart = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A5").Value + 1
   ZeileEnde = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1
   
Set rngBereich = Range(Cells(ZeileStart, 3), Cells(ZeileEnde, 3))
      
If Not Intersect(Range(Target.Address), rngBereich) Is Nothing Then

If Target.Font.ColorIndex = 50 Then ' Farbe GrÃžn
    Target.Font.Color = -5211136 'Farbe Blau
    End If
 
End If

''' PrÃžfung Fahrzeugbeschriftung
'''
On Error Resume Next

If Not Intersect(Target, Range("K32")) Is Nothing Then
   
        If Target.Value = "" Then
        Target.Select
        Call Beschriftung_prÃžfen_lÃķschen1
        Else
        If Target.Value = "NEIN" Then
        Call Beschriftung_prÃžfen_lÃķschen1
        Else
        If Target.Value = "JA" Then
        Call Beschriftung_prÃžfen_lÃķschen1
        Call Beschriftung_prÃžfen1
        End If
        End If
        End If
End If

If Not Intersect(Target, Range("M33")) Is Nothing Then
   
        If Target.Value = "" Then
        Target.Cells.Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        Target.Cells.Offset(2, 0).Value = ""
        Target.Select
        Call Beschriftung_prÃžfen_lÃķschen2
        Else
        If Target.Value = "NEIN" Then
        Target.Cells.Offset(1, 0).Value = "---"
        Target.Cells.Offset(2, 0).Value = "---"
        Call Beschriftung_prÃžfen_lÃķschen2
        Else
        If Target.Value = "JA" Then
        Target.Cells.Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        Target.Cells.Offset(2, 0).Value = ""
        Call Beschriftung_prÃžfen_lÃķschen2
        Call Beschriftung_prÃžfen2
        End If
        End If
        End If
End If

If Not Intersect(Target, Range("M34")) Is Nothing Then
        If Target.Value = "" Then
        Target.Cells.Offset(-1, 0).Value = ""
        Target.Cells.Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        Target.Select
        Else
        If Target.Cells.Offset(-1, 0).Value = "NEIN" Then
        Target.Value = "---"
        Else
        If Target.Value = "Kunde" Then
        Target.Cells.Offset(1, 0).Value = "---"
        Else
        If Target.Value = "MU" Then
        Target.Cells.Offset(1, 0).Value = "=today()+14"
        Target.Select
        End If
        End If
        End If
        End If
End If

        If Target.Value = "" Then
        Target.Cells.Offset(-2, 0).Value = ""
        Target.Cells.Offset(-1, 0).Value = ""

        Else

        Target.Value = "---"
        Else
        If Target.Cells.Offset(-1, 0).Value = "Kunde" Then
        Target.Value = "---"

        End If
        End If

On Error Resume Next

 'If Target.Address = "$S$3" Then

    ''''''' Es wird geprÃžft welcher Aufbautyp in F4 eingetragen wurde.

    ''''''' Bei Nichtverwendung bitte:

    ''''''' Makro PrÃžfung_SeitlWassertanks (siehe unten) lÃķschen
    ''''''' Makro PrÃžfung_SeitlWassertanks_lÃķschen (siehe unten) lÃķschen
    ''''
    
    If Range("F4") Like "*Prof*" Or _
        Range("F4") Like "*Pro*" Or _
        Range("F4") Like "*type II*" Or _
        Range("F4") Like "*typ II*" Or _
        Range("F4") Like "*Typ 2*" Or _
        Range("F4") Like "*type 2*" Or _
        Range("F4") Like "*Typ II*" Then
        
    Call PrÃžfung_SeitlWassertanks_lÃķschen ' Makro siehe unten
    Call PrÃžfung_SeitlWassertanks ' Makro siehe unten
    Else
    Call PrÃžfung_SeitlWassertanks_lÃķschen ' siehe Makro unten
    End If

    Call RAP_prÃžfen 'Modul14   prÃžft ob Dateilbereits vorhanden

End If

''' Code fÃžr die Bedingte Formatierung im Bereich Fahrzeugbeleuchtung

Dim r As Long

If Application.ScreenUpdating = True Then Application.ScreenUpdating = False

    For r = 69 To Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A4").Value - 1
        If InStr(Cells(r, 10).Value, "") Then
            Range(Cells(r, 10), Cells(r, 10)).Interior.Color = xlNone
            Else

        End If

            Else

            Else
            Range(Cells(r, 21), Cells(r, 21)).Interior.Color = RGB(235, 241, 222)
        End If

'''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''
''In dieser Funktion wird der BW_Text immer eine Zeile weiter markiert.
''
On Error Resume Next

Dim HÃķhe As Single

If Not Intersect(Target, Range("BW")) Is Nothing Then
       
        If Target.Offset(1, -22).Value = "" Then
        ActiveCell.Offset(0, -5).Activate
        ActiveWorkbook.Names.Add Name:="AktiveZeile", RefersToR1C1:=Target.Row
        Target.Interior.ColorIndex = xlNone
        GoTo EndeBW
        Else
                If Target.Offset(1, 0).Value = "" Then
                Target.Interior.ColorIndex = xlNone
                Target.Cells.Offset(1, 0).Select
                Else
                Target.Interior.ColorIndex = xlNone
                Target.Select
                GoTo EndeBW
                End If
        End If


        If Target.Offset(1, 0).RowHeight > Target.Offset(1, 0).Top - Target.Top Then
        HÃķhe = Target.Offset(1, 0).RowHeight / 16
        Else
        HÃķhe = 0
        End If
    
        With ActiveSheet.Shapes("BW_Text")
            .Visible = True
            ' Oberkante=Oberkante der geklickten Zelle
        .Top = Target.Top + Target.RowHeight + HÃķhe
            ' linke Kante=linke Kante der rechten Nachbarzelle
        .Left = Target.Offset(0, 1).Left
        End With

EndeBW:

End If

'''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''''


On Error Resume Next
''' Hier wird geprÃžft ob unter der vorletzten Zeile im Bereich Technische Ãnderungen "LastRow2" steht.
''' Dann wir das Makro Zeile einfÃžgen gestartet.
''' Damit ist sichergestellt das automatisch beim fÃžllen der vorletzten Zeile eine neu eingefÃžgt wird.

If Target.Cells.Offset(2, 0).Value = "LastRow2" Then
    Target.Cells.Offset(1, 0).Select
    Call Zeile_einfÃžgen
End If

Call Zaehler '(Modul 5)

Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

Private Sub PrÃžfung_SeitlWassertanks()

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

On Error Resume Next

   Dim rngBereich As Range
   Dim c As Range
   Dim ZeileStart As Integer
   Dim ZeileEnde As Integer
   
   ZeileStart = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A5").Value + 1
   ZeileEnde = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1
   
   Set rngBereich = Range(Cells(ZeileStart, 3), Cells(ZeileEnde, 3))
      
   For Each c In rngBereich
      If IsEmpty(c) Or c = "" Then
         c.Value = "Seitliche Wassertanks mit Verkleidungsblech JA / NEIN ?"
         c.Font.Color = -10053325 'Farbe GrÃžn
         Exit For
      End If
   Next c
   
Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

Private Sub PrÃžfung_SeitlWassertanks_lÃķschen()

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

On Error Resume Next

   Dim rngBereich As Range
   Dim c As Range
   Dim ZeileStart As Integer
   Dim ZeileEnde As Integer
   
   ZeileStart = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A5").Value + 1
   ZeileEnde = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1
   
   Set rngBereich = Range(Cells(ZeileStart, 3), Cells(ZeileEnde, 3))
      
   For Each c In rngBereich
      If c.Value = "Seitliche Wassertanks mit Verkleidungsblech JA / NEIN ?" Then
         c.Value = ""
         c.Font.Color = -5211136 'Farbe Blau
     End If
   Next c
   
Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

Private Sub UserForm_Initialize()

On Error Resume Next

'''' Legt die Position der Userform fest.

        StartUpPosition = 0
        With Application
        .WindowState = xlMaximized
        Me.Top = Application.Top
        Me.Left = Application.Left
        Me.Height = Application.Height
        Me.Width = Application.Width
        End With


        hwndForm = FindWindow(GC_CLASSNAMEMSEXCELFORM, Me.Caption)

        If hwndForm <> 0 Then
        SetWindowLong hwndForm, GWL_STYLE, GetWindowLong(hwndForm, GWL_STYLE) And Not WS_CAPTION
        DrawMenuBar hwndForm
        End If
        
        Image1.Picture = LoadPicture("U:\Bilder_RAP\Aufbautyp\1.jpg")
        Image2.Picture = LoadPicture("U:\Bilder_RAP\Aufbautyp\2.jpg")
        Image3.Picture = LoadPicture("U:\Bilder_RAP\Aufbautyp\3.jpg")
        Image4.Picture = LoadPicture("U:\Bilder_RAP\Aufbautyp\4.jpg")
        Image5.Picture = LoadPicture("U:\Bilder_RAP\Aufbautyp\5.jpg")
        Image6.Picture = LoadPicture("U:\Bilder_RAP\Aufbautyp\6.jpg")
        Image7.Picture = LoadPicture("U:\Bilder_RAP\Aufbautyp\7.jpg")
        Image8.Picture = LoadPicture("U:\Bilder_RAP\Aufbautyp\8.jpg")
        Image9.Picture = LoadPicture("U:\Bilder_RAP\Aufbautyp\9.jpg")
        Image10.Picture = LoadPicture("U:\Bilder_RAP\Aufbautyp\10.jpg")
        Image11.Picture = LoadPicture("U:\Bilder_RAP\Aufbautyp\11.jpg")
        
End Sub

Option Explicit
Sub Aufbautyp1()
   Dim strPfad As String
   Dim pic As Picture
   strPfad = "U:\Bilder_RAP\1.png"
   If Dir(strPfad) = "" Then Exit Sub
   Set pic = ActiveSheet.Pictures.Insert(strPfad)
   
   With ActiveSheet.Range("B55")
   ' Abstand links und oben
       pic.Left = .Left + 2
       pic.Top = .Top
       pic.BringToFront
       pic.OnAction = "Aufbautyp_Schutz"
   End With
   
Range("J69").Select
Call Cursor_Position_Aufbautyp 'Modul 11

End Sub

   If Dir(strPfad) = "" Then Exit Sub
   Set pic = ActiveSheet.Pictures.Insert(strPfad)
   
   With ActiveSheet.Range("B55")
   ' Abstand links und oben
       pic.Left = .Left + 2
       pic.Top = .Top
       pic.BringToFront
       pic.OnAction = "Aufbautyp_Schutz"
   End With
   
Range("J69").Select
Call Cursor_Position_Aufbautyp 'Modul 11

End Sub
Sub Aufbautyp11()
   Dim strPfad As String
   Dim pic As Picture
   strPfad = "U:\Bilder_RAP\11.png"
   If Dir(strPfad) = "" Then Exit Sub
   Set pic = ActiveSheet.Pictures.Insert(strPfad)
   
   With ActiveSheet.Range("B55")
   ' Abstand links und oben
       pic.Left = .Left + 2
       pic.Top = .Top
       pic.BringToFront
       pic.OnAction = "Aufbautyp_Schutz"
   End With
   
Range("J69").Select
Call Cursor_Position_Aufbautyp 'Modul 11

End Sub

Private Sub cblÃķsch_Click()
Dim i As String
Dim AktivesBlatt As Variant
Dim shp As Shape
Dim Bilddatei As String
Dim Zelle As Range

AktivesBlatt = ActiveSheet.Name

Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Application.EnableEvents = False

On Error Resume Next


Zelle = ActiveCell

For Each shp In ActiveSheet.Shapes
If shp.TopLeftCell.Row = ActiveCell.Row Then
            shp.Delete
        End If
    Next shp

Zelle.Select

Bilddatei = ActiveCell.Offset(0, 22).Value

For Each shp In ActiveSheet.Shapes
If shp.Name = Bilddatei Then
            shp.Delete
        End If
    Next shp

Range(Cells(ActiveCell.Row, 3), Cells(ActiveCell.Row, 31)).ClearContents 'Der Inhalt von der Aktiven Zeile wird von Spalte 3 bis  geleert
Range(Cells(ActiveCell.Row, 35), Cells(ActiveCell.Row, 39)).ClearContents

If ActiveCell.Value = "" Then
ActiveCell.Interior.Color = RGB(235, 241, 222)
Else
ActiveCell.Interior.Color = xlNone
End If

Application.EnableEvents = True

ActiveCell.Offset(0, 1).Value = ""
ActiveCell.Offset(0, 1).Select

Unload UserForm1

End Sub

Private Sub Label_Click()
On Error Resume Next
With Label
If .Caption = VBA.Chr(168) Then .Caption = VBA.Chr(254) Else .Caption = VBA.Chr(168)
End With
If Label.Caption = VBA.Chr(254) Then
UserForm1.TextBox_Grafik.Enabled = True
UserForm1.Label4.Enabled = True
UserForm1.SpinButton.Enabled = True
Else
UserForm1.TextBox_Grafik.Enabled = False
UserForm1.Label4.Enabled = False
UserForm1.SpinButton.Enabled = False
End If
End Sub

 End If

 End If

Sub UserForm_Initialize()

Dim sText As String
Dim i As Integer
Dim intIndex1
Dim intIndex2


Application.EnableEvents = True

On Error Resume Next

 hwndForm = FindWindow(GC_CLASSNAMEMSEXCELFORM, Me.Caption)

   If hwndForm <> 0 Then
        SetWindowLong hwndForm, GWL_STYLE, GetWindowLong(hwndForm, GWL_STYLE) And Not WS_CAPTION
        DrawMenuBar hwndForm
    End If
    
    
StartUpPosition = 0
    With Application
        .WindowState = xlMaximized
        Left = .Left + .Width / 2 - Width / 2
        Top = .Top + .Height / 2 - Height / 2
    End With
    

Label.Caption = VBA.Chr(168)
UserForm1.TextBox_Grafik.Enabled = False
UserForm1.Label4.Enabled = False
UserForm1.SpinButton.Enabled = False
SpinButton.Value = 1
SpinButton.Max = 10
SpinButton.Min = 1
SpinButton.SmallChange = 1
TextBox_Grafik.Locked = True


If Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A1").Value = "1" Then
For i = 1 To Sheets("FZB").Cells(1, Cells.Columns.Count).End(xlToLeft).Column
    ListBox1.AddItem Sheets("FZB").Cells(1, i)
Next
Else
For i = 1 To Sheets("FZB").Cells(20, Cells.Columns.Count).End(xlToLeft).Column
    ListBox1.AddItem Sheets("FZB").Cells(20, i)
    
Next
End If

If ActiveCell.Offset(0, 17).Value = "" Then
ListBox1.ListIndex = 0
Else
ListBox1.ListIndex = ActiveCell.Offset(0, 17).Value
    If ActiveCell.Offset(0, 18).Value = "" Then
    ListBox1.ListIndex = 0
    Else
    ListBox2.ListIndex = ActiveCell.Offset(0, 18).Value
    End If
TextBox1.Text = ActiveCell.Value
Label6.Visible = True
Label6.Caption = ActiveCell.Offset(0, 24).Value & "."
End If

If ActiveCell.Offset(0, 17).Value = "6" Then
Label6.Visible = False
Label7.Visible = True
Label7.Caption = ActiveCell.Offset(0, 24).Value & "."
ElseIf ActiveCell.Offset(0, 17).Value = "11" Then
Label6.Visible = False
Label7.Visible = True
Label7.Caption = ActiveCell.Offset(0, 24).Value & "."
Else
Label6.Visible = True
Label7.Visible = False
End If

If ListBox1.ListIndex = 0 Then
 UserForm1.Image1.Picture = Tabelle11.ASW1.Picture
 End If
If ListBox1.ListIndex = 1 Then
 UserForm1.Image1.Picture = Tabelle11.FHB1.Picture
End If
 If ListBox1.ListIndex = 2 Then
 UserForm1.Image1.Picture = Tabelle11.RUK1.Picture
 End If
 If ListBox1.ListIndex = 3 Then
 UserForm1.Image1.Picture = Tabelle11.SPO1.Picture
 End If
 If ListBox1.ListIndex = 4 Then
 UserForm1.Image1.Picture = Tabelle11.ASW1.Picture
 End If
 If ListBox1.ListIndex = 5 Then
 UserForm1.Image1.Picture = Tabelle11.ASW1.Picture
 End If
 If ListBox1.ListIndex = 6 Then
 UserForm1.Image1.Picture = Tabelle11.LED1.Picture
 End If
 If ListBox1.ListIndex = 7 Then
 UserForm1.Image1.Picture = Tabelle11.RFK1.Picture
 End If
 If ListBox1.ListIndex = 8 Then

Private Sub cbok_Click()
Dim i As Integer
Dim auswahl As Long
Dim lngCnt As Long
Dim txt As String

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False


ActiveCell.Offset(0, 13).ClearContents
ActiveCell.Offset(0, 14).ClearContents

lngCnt = 13

ActiveCell = ""
For auswahl = 0 To ListBox1.ListCount - 1
       If ListBox1.Selected(auswahl) = True Then
       ActiveCell = IIf(ActiveCell = "", ListBox1.List(auswahl), ActiveCell & vbLf & ListBox1.List(auswahl))
       txt = ListBox1.List(auswahl)
       ActiveCell.Offset(0, lngCnt).Value = txt
       lngCnt = lngCnt + 1
       End If
Next

If ActiveCell.Offset(0, 13).Value = "RÃžckwÃĪrtsgang" And ActiveCell.Offset(0, 11).Value = "Rundumkennleuchten" Then
MsgBox "Diese Auswahl ist nicht mÃķglich!", vbCritical
ActiveCell.Value = ""
End If

If ActiveCell.Offset(0, 14).Value = "RÃžckwÃĪrtsgang" And ActiveCell.Offset(0, 11).Value = "Rundumkennleuchten" Then
MsgBox "Diese Auswahl ist nicht mÃķglich!", vbCritical
ActiveCell.Value = ""
End If

If ActiveCell.Offset(0, 13).Value = "RÃžckwÃĪrtsgang" And ActiveCell.Offset(0, 11).Value = "Front- und Heckblitzer" Then
MsgBox "Diese Auswahl ist nicht mÃķglich!", vbCritical
ActiveCell.Value = ""
End If

If ActiveCell.Offset(0, 14).Value = "RÃžckwÃĪrtsgang" And ActiveCell.Offset(0, 11).Value = "Front- und Heckblitzer" Then
MsgBox "Diese Auswahl ist nicht mÃķglich!", vbCritical
ActiveCell.Value = ""
End If

If ActiveCell.Value = "" Then
ActiveCell.Interior.Color = RGB(235, 241, 222)
Else
ActiveCell.Interior.Color = xlNone
End If

Unload UserForm2

ActiveCell.Offset(0, -1).Select

Call UserForm3_open ' Modul 13

Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

Private Sub ListBox1_Change()
Dim iInd%
Dim i As Integer, Cnt As Integer

Cnt = 0
iInd = ListBox1.ListIndex
For i = 0 To ListBox1.ListCount - 1
If ListBox1.Selected(i) = True Then
Cnt = Cnt + 1
End If
Next i
If Cnt > 2 Then
ListBox1.Selected(iInd) = False
MsgBox "Die Auswahl ist auf 2 begrenzt!"
End If
End Sub

     End With

Else
For i = 45 To 51
    ListBox1.AddItem Sheets("1").Cells(i, 2)
Next
End If

End Sub

VBA MACRO Modul1.bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Modul1'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Option Explicit

Sub ZeilenhoeheVerbundene(lngZeileNr As Long)
'  Parameter ist die Zeilennummer.
'  In einer Zeile kann es mehrere verbundene Zellen geben.
   Dim sngHoehe As Single, cc As Integer, rngC As Range
   Dim sngActWid As Single, rngM As Range, sngMergWid As Single

   Application.ScreenUpdating = False
   With Rows(lngZeileNr)
      .AutoFit
      sngHoehe = .RowHeight + 3 ' MindesthÃķhe (insbes. nicht-verbundene Zellen)
   End With
   For cc = 1 To Cells(lngZeileNr, Columns.Count).End(xlToLeft).Column
      If Cells(lngZeileNr, cc) > "" And Cells(lngZeileNr, cc).MergeCells Then
         Set rngC = Cells(lngZeileNr, cc)
         If Len(rngC) > 1000 Then
            MsgBox "Der Text in " & rngC.Address(0, 0) & " hat Ãžber 1000 Zeichen !" _
               & vbLf & vbLf & "Bitte kÃžrzen!", vbCritical, "ZeilenhoeheVerbundene"
            rngC.Select
            Exit Sub
         End If
         With rngC.MergeArea
            If .Cells(1).Address = rngC.Address And .WrapText = True Then
               sngActWid = rngC.ColumnWidth      ' Merken zum Wiederherstellen
               ' ---------------------------------------- Gesamtbreite rechnen
               For Each rngM In .Cells
                  sngMergWid = rngM.ColumnWidth + sngMergWid
               Next
               sngMergWid = sngMergWid + (.Count - 1) * 0.71
               ' ----------------- Merge aufheben, Zellbreite auf Gesamtbreite
               .MergeCells = False
               rngC.ColumnWidth = sngMergWid
               ' ---------------------------------- max. optim. HÃķhe ermitteln
               .EntireRow.AutoFit
               sngHoehe = Application.Max(sngHoehe, rngC.Height)
               ' --------------------------- Breite und Merge wiederherstellen
               rngC.ColumnWidth = sngActWid
               .MergeCells = True
            End If
         End With
      End If
   Next cc
   Rows(lngZeileNr).RowHeight = sngHoehe        ' max. optim. HÃķhe einstellen
   
  
  'Application.ScreenUpdating = True
  
  
End Sub

Sub Zeile_einfÃžgen()
Dim i As String
Dim AktivesBlatt As Variant
Dim shp As Shape

Dim ZeileStartB1 As Integer
Dim ZeileEndeB1 As Integer
Dim ZeileStartB2 As Integer
Dim ZeileEndeB2 As Integer
Dim SpalteStart1 As Integer
Dim SpalteEnde1 As Integer
Dim SpalteStart2 As Integer
Dim SpalteEnde2 As Integer

Dim Bereich1, Bereich2, myMultipleRange As Range

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

ActiveSheet.Shapes("BW_Text").Left = Cells(22, 37).Left
ActiveSheet.Shapes("BW_Text").Top = Cells(22, 37).Top
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Preis_Text").Left = Cells(30, 37).Left
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Preis_Text").Top = Cells(30, 37).Top

On Error Resume Next

Worksheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Activate

ZeileStartB1 = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A3").Value + 1
ZeileEndeB1 = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A4").Value - 1
ZeileStartB2 = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A5").Value + 1
ZeileEndeB2 = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1


SpalteStart1 = 3
SpalteEnde1 = 25
SpalteStart2 = 3
SpalteEnde2 = 62

Set Bereich1 = Range(Cells(ZeileStartB1, SpalteStart1), Cells(ZeileEndeB1, SpalteEnde1))
Set Bereich2 = Range(Cells(ZeileStartB2, SpalteStart2), Cells(ZeileEndeB2, SpalteEnde2))
Set myMultipleRange = Union(Bereich1, Bereich2)

i = ActiveCell.Row

If Not Intersect(Range(ActiveCell.Address), myMultipleRange) Is Nothing Then

Rows(CDbl(i)).Select
Selection.Copy
Selection.Insert Shift:=xlDown
Selection.PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteFormats, Operation:=xlNone, _
SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
ActiveSheet.Rows(i + 0).Select  'in die neu eingefÃžgte Zelle springen
Range(Cells(ActiveCell.Row, 3), Cells(ActiveCell.Row, 31)).ClearContents 'Der Inhalt von der Aktiven Zeile wird von Spalte 3 bis 31 geleert
ActiveCell.Select 'und den Bereich "A" der aktiven Zeile auswÃĪhlen
ActiveCell.Offset(0, 9).Select
For Each shp In ActiveSheet.Shapes
If shp.TopLeftCell.Row = ActiveCell.Row Then
            shp.Delete
        End If
    Next shp
Else
MsgBox "In diesem Bereich ist das EinfÃžgen einer Zeile nicht mÃķglich !", vbCritical, "Warnung"
End If

If ActiveCell.Interior.Color = RGB(235, 241, 222) Then
ActiveCell.Offset(0, -7).Interior.Color = RGB(235, 241, 222)
Else
ActiveCell.Offset(0, -7).Interior.Color = xlNone
End If

Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub
Sub Zeile_lÃķschen()
'In diesem Makro wird der Bereich geprÃžft in der die Zeile gelÃķscht werden soll
'Im 2. Makro "Zeile_lÃķschen_bereich" Makro wird ein Zweiter Bereich geprÃžft
'Im 3a. Makro "Zeile_lÃķschen_oben" wird die Zeile im oberen Bereich (Bereich1) gelÃķscht. Dort sind Shapes enthalten
'Im 3b. Makro "Zeile_lÃķschen_unten" wird die Zeile im unteren Bereich (Bereich2) gelÃķscht.

Dim ZeileStartB1 As Integer
Dim ZeileEndeB1 As Integer
Dim ZeileStartB2 As Integer
Dim ZeileEndeB2 As Integer
Dim SpalteStart As Integer
Dim SpalteEnde As Integer

Dim Bereich1, Bereich2, myMultipleRange As Range


Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

ActiveSheet.Shapes("BW_Text").Left = Cells(22, 37).Left
ActiveSheet.Shapes("BW_Text").Top = Cells(22, 37).Top
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Preis_Text").Left = Cells(30, 37).Left
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Preis_Text").Top = Cells(30, 37).Top

Worksheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Activate

ZeileStartB1 = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A3").Value + 1
ZeileEndeB1 = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A4").Value - 2
ZeileStartB2 = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A5").Value + 2
ZeileEndeB2 = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 2

SpalteStart = 3
SpalteEnde = 25

Set Bereich1 = Range(Cells(ZeileStartB1, SpalteStart), Cells(ZeileEndeB1, SpalteEnde))
Set Bereich2 = Range(Cells(ZeileStartB2, SpalteStart), Cells(ZeileEndeB2, SpalteEnde))
Set myMultipleRange = Union(Bereich1, Bereich2)

If Not Intersect(Range(ActiveCell.Address), myMultipleRange) Is Nothing Then
Call Zeile_lÃķschen_bereich
Else
MsgBox "Zeile lÃķschen nicht mÃķglich !" & vbLf & _
 "Der Inhalt der Zeile kann gelÃķscht werden.", vbCritical, "Warnung"
Application.EnableEvents = True
End If

End Sub
Sub Zeile_lÃķschen_bereich()
'In diesem Makro wird der Bereich geprÃžft in der die Zeile gelÃķscht werden soll (oben oder unten)

Dim ZeileStartB As Integer
Dim ZeileEndeB As Integer
Dim ZeileStartB2 As Integer
Dim ZeileEndeB2 As Integer
Dim SpalteStart As Integer
Dim SpalteEnde As Integer

Dim Bereich As Range

Application.EnableEvents = False

ActiveSheet.Shapes("BW_Text").Left = Cells(22, 37).Left
ActiveSheet.Shapes("BW_Text").Top = Cells(22, 37).Top
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Preis_Text").Left = Cells(30, 37).Left
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Preis_Text").Top = Cells(30, 37).Top

SpalteEnde = 25

If Not Intersect(Range(ActiveCell.Address), Bereich) Is Nothing Then
Call Zeile_lÃķschen_oben
Else

End If

End Sub
Sub Zeile_lÃķschen_oben()
'Makro 3a.
Dim i As String

ActiveSheet.Shapes("Preis_Text").Top = Cells(30, 37).Top

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

ActiveCell.Offset(0, 11).Select

For Each shp In ActiveSheet.Shapes
If shp.TopLeftCell.Row = ActiveCell.Row Then
            shp.Delete
        End If
    Next shp

Bilddatei = ActiveCell.Value

For Each shp In ActiveSheet.Shapes
If shp.Name = Bilddatei Then
            shp.Delete
        End If
    Next shp

i = ActiveCell.Row
Rows(CDbl(i)).Select
Rows(CDbl(i)).Delete Shift:=xlUp
ActiveCell.Select 'und den Bereich "A" der aktiven Zeile auswÃĪhlen
ActiveCell.Offset(0, 9).Select
Application.EnableEvents = True
'Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

Option Explicit
Sub Shape_Tabelle_einfÃžgen_umbenennen()

Dim Bild As Shape
Dim Zelle As Range
Dim Name As Integer

On Error Resume Next

Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Application.EnableEvents = False

    ActiveCell.Offset(0, -1).Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    ActiveCell.Offset(0, 1).Select
    ActiveCell.Offset(0, -1).Select

With ActiveSheet
Set Bild = .Shapes(.Shapes.Count)
Set Zelle = ActiveCell
End With
   
If ActiveCell.Offset(0, 23).Value = "0" Then
Bild.Top = Zelle.Top + (Zelle.Height - Bild.Height) / 2
Bild.Left = Zelle.Left + (Zelle.Width - Bild.Width) / 2
Else
Bild.Top = Zelle.Top + 7
Bild.Left = Zelle.Left + (Zelle.Width - Bild.Width) / 2
End If

Bild.Select
Selection.Formula = "=" & ActiveCell.Offset(0, 31).AddressLocal
Selection.Name = Selection.Name & ActiveCell.Offset(0, 31).Value
ActiveCell.Offset(0, 28).Value = Selection.Name

If ActiveCell.Offset(0, 1).Value = "" Then
ActiveCell.Offset(0, 1).Interior.Color = RGB(235, 241, 222)
Else
ActiveCell.Offset(0, 1).Interior.Color = xlNone
End If

If ActiveCell.Offset(0, 26).Value = "JA" Then
Call Shape_Position_einfÃžgen_umbenennen
Else
        If ActiveCell.Offset(2, 1).Value = "LastRow1" Then
        ActiveCell.Offset(1, 1).Select
        Application.ScreenUpdating = False
        Call Zeile_einfÃžgen
        ActiveCell.Offset(0, -5).Select
        ElseIf ActiveCell.Offset(1, 1).Value = "" Then
        Application.ScreenUpdating = False
        ActiveCell.Offset(1, 1).Select
        Else
        ActiveCell.Offset(0, 9).Select
        Application.ScreenUpdating = False
        Unload UserForm1
        Call UserForm3_open ' Modul 13
        End If
End If

Application.ScreenUpdating = True
Application.EnableEvents = True

End Sub
Sub Shape_Position_einfÃžgen_umbenennen()

Dim Zelle As Range

On Error Resume Next

 ElseIf ActiveCell.Offset(0, 24).Value = "1" Then

 ElseIf ActiveCell.Offset(0, 24).Value = "6" Then

 ElseIf ActiveCell.Offset(0, 24).Value = "7" Then

 ElseIf ActiveCell.Offset(0, 24).Value = "8" Then

 ElseIf ActiveCell.Offset(0, 24).Value = "10" Then

 ElseIf ActiveCell.Offset(0, 24).Value = "11" Then

 ElseIf ActiveCell.Offset(0, 24).Value = "12" Then
  Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Shapes("RBL0").Copy

anzahl = ActiveCell.Offset(0, 27).Value

With ActiveSheet

Set Zelle = ActiveCell
End With

For i = 1 To anzahl

Zelle.Offset(0, 29).Value = Selection.Name

VBA MACRO Modul5.bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Modul5'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Option Explicit
Sub selektieren()
Dim ZeileStart As Integer
Dim ZeileEnde As Long
Dim i As Long

On Error Resume Next


ZeileStart = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A5").Value + 1
ZeileEnde = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1

For i = ZeileStart To ZeileEnde
    If Cells(i, 3).Value <> "" Then
    Cells(i, 24) = "X"
    End If
Next i

Call Zaehler

End Sub
Sub Zaehler()
Dim ZeileStart As Integer
Dim ZeileEnde As Integer
Dim Bereich1 As Range
Dim Spalte1 As Integer
Dim Ergebnis1 As Integer
Dim Bereich2 As Range
Dim Spalte2 As Integer
Dim Ergebnis2 As Integer

Dim Zeile1 As Integer
Dim Zeile2 As Integer

Dim Zelle As Integer

On Error Resume Next

Zelle = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A1").Value

ZeileStart = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A5").Value + 1
ZeileEnde = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1

Spalte1 = 3
Spalte2 = 24


Set Bereich1 = Range(Cells(ZeileStart, Spalte1), Cells(ZeileEnde, Spalte1)) ' Bereich der Wirksamkeit
Set Bereich2 = Range(Cells(ZeileStart, Spalte2), Cells(ZeileEnde, Spalte2)) ' Bereich der Wirksamkeit

Ergebnis1 = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(Bereich1, "<>")
Ergebnis2 = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(Bereich2, "<>")

If Ergebnis1 > Ergebnis2 Then
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Teilfreigabe").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
    If Zelle = 1 Then
    ActiveSheet.Shapes("D_X").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
    Else
    ActiveSheet.Shapes("E_X").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
    End If
End If

If Ergebnis1 = Ergebnis2 Then
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Kompl._Freigabe").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
    If Zelle = 1 Then
    ActiveSheet.Shapes("D_all").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
    Else
    ActiveSheet.Shapes("E_all").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
    End If
End If

If Ergebnis1 > 0 And Ergebnis2 = 0 Then
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Keine_Freigabe").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Blanko").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
End If

If Ergebnis1 = 0 And Ergebnis2 = 0 Then
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Leer").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Blanko").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
End If

If Ergebnis2 > Ergebnis1 Then
ActiveSheet.Shapes("Leer").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
MsgBox "Mehr Freigaben als Technische Ãnderungen nicht mÃķglich!", vbCritical
ActiveCell.Offset(0, 4).Value = ""
End If

End Sub
Sub Kundenfreigabe_speichern()

Dim ZeileStart As Integer
Dim SpalteStart As Integer
Dim ZeileEnde As Integer
Dim SpalteEnde As Integer
Dim Zelle As Integer

Dim i As Long

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

Call Netzwerkstatus 'Modul 5

If ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "NEIN" Then
GoTo ende
End If

Zelle = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A1").Value
ZeileStart = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A5").Value + 1
ZeileEnde = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1

Application.EnableEvents = False

For i = ZeileStart To ZeileEnde
    If Cells(i, 3).Value <> "" And Cells(i, 24) = "X" Then
    Cells(i, 24).Font.Name = "Wingdings 2"
    Cells(i, 24).Value = "P"
    ElseIf Cells(i, 3).Value <> "" And Cells(i, 24) = "" Then
    Cells(i, 24).Value = "X"
    End If
Next i

ActiveSheet.Shapes("Leer").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)

If Zelle = 1 Then
    ActiveSheet.Shapes("D_X_frei").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
    Else
    ActiveSheet.Shapes("E_X_frei").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)
End If

Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

Call Kundenfreigabe_speichern_pdf

ende:

End Sub
Sub Kundenfreigabe_speichern_pdf()


Dim Projektpfad As String
Dim xlOpenAfterPublish As Boolean

Dim Pfad As String, Nummer As Integer, Dateinummer As String
Dim Dateiname As String

Dim Antwort As Integer

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

ActiveSheet.Shapes("Leer").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)

Dateiname = "RAP_" & Range("S3") & "_("

Pfad = ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value
    
Projektpfad = Dir(Pfad)
Do While Projektpfad <> ""
If VBA.Left(Projektpfad, 14) = Dateiname Then
If Nummer < CInt(VBA.Mid(Projektpfad, 15, 2)) Then Nummer = CInt(VBA.Mid(Projektpfad, 15, 2))
End If
Projektpfad = Dir
Loop
Dateinummer = String(2 - Len(CStr(Nummer + 1)), "0") & CStr(Nummer + 1)


Dateiname = "RAP_" & Range("S3") & "_(" & Dateinummer & ")_K.pdf"


'PDF-Ãffnen-Abfrage erstellen
Antwort = MsgBox("Soll die PDF-Datei nach dem Erstellen angezeigt werden?", vbYesNoCancel + vbQuestion, "Frage")

If Antwort = vbYes Then
xlOpenAfterPublish = True
GoTo Weiter
End If

If Antwort = vbNo Then
GoTo Weiter
End If

If Antwort = vbCancel Then
GoTo ende
End If

Weiter:

ActiveSheet.Shapes("Leer").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)

ActiveSheet.ExportAsFixedFormat Type:=xlTypePDF, Filename:=Pfad & Dateiname _
 , Quality:=xlQualityStandard, IncludeDocProperties:=True, IgnorePrintAreas:=False, OpenAfterPublish:=IIf(xlOpenAfterPublish, True, False)

'Boolean-Variable einschalten
xlOpenAfterPublish = True

Application.ScreenUpdating = False

If UserForm3.Visible = True Then
Call UserForm3.OpenFiles 'Modul 13
End If

ende:

ActiveSheet.Shapes("Leer").ZOrder (msoBringToFront)

Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

Call Kundenfreigabe_alt

End Sub
Sub Kundenfreigabe_alt()

Dim ZeileStart As Integer
Dim SpalteStart As Integer
Dim ZeileEnde As Integer
Dim SpalteEnde As Integer
Dim Zelle As Range

Dim i As Long

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

ZeileStart = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A5").Value + 1
ZeileEnde = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1

Set Zelle = Range(Cells(ZeileStart, 3), Cells(ZeileStart, 20))

For i = ZeileStart To ZeileEnde
    If Cells(i, 3).Value <> "" And Cells(i, 24) = "X" Then
    Cells(i, 24) = ""
    ElseIf Cells(i, 3).Value <> "" And Cells(i, 24).Font.Name = "Wingdings 2" Then
    Cells(i, 24).Font.Name = "Arial"
    Cells(i, 24).Value = "X"
    End If
Next i

Zelle.Select

Call Zaehler

Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub
Sub Kundenfreigabe_versenden()

Dim App   As Object
Dim Dateiname As String
Dim Projektpfad As String
Dim isNew As Boolean
Dim thema As String
Dim AWS As String

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

On Error GoTo Fehler

Projektpfad = ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value
Dateiname = UserForm3.ListBox1.Value

If Not UserForm3.ListBox1.Value Like "*K*" Then
MsgBox ("Diese Datei kann nicht versendet werden.") & vbLf & vbLf & ("Bitte eine .pdf Datei fÃžr Kundenfreigabe auswÃĪhlen."), vbInformation
GoTo ende
End If

On Error Resume Next
   Set App = GetObject(, "Outlook.Application")
   If App Is Nothing Then
      Set App = CreateObject("Outlook.Application")
      isNew = True
   End If

With App.CreateItem(0)
.GetInspector ' sorgt fÃžr die Signatur
.To = ""
.Subject = ""
.Attachments.Add Projektpfad & Dateiname
.Display
End With

GoTo ende

Fehler:
MsgBox ("Keine Datei ausgewÃĪhlt.") & vbLf & vbLf & ("Bitte eine .pdf Datei fÃžr Kundenfreigabe auswÃĪhlen."), vbInformation

ende:

Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

Option Explicit
Private Function DateiGeoeffnet(DerPfad As String) As Boolean
' Bei shared Workbooks, schreibgeschÃžtzten Mappen o.ÃĪ.. kann dies auch ein falsch zurÃžckgeben.
    On Error Resume Next
    Open DerPfad For Binary Access Read Lock Read As #1
    Close #1
    If Err.Number <> 0 Then
        DateiGeoeffnet = True
        Err.Clear
    End If
End Function

Sub Deutsch_Englisch()

Dim find_str As String, repl_str As String
Dim repl_arr As Variant

Dim Zeile As Integer

Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Application.EnableEvents = False

On Error Resume Next

GoTo ende

GoTo ende
End If

If ActiveSheet.Range("A1").Value = 2 Then
GoTo ende
End If

Dateiname = "RAP_" & Range("S3") & "_E" & ".xlsm"

Pfad = ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value

If Dir(Pfad & Dateiname) <> "" Then
    sPfad = Pfad & Dateiname
    If DateiGeoeffnet(sPfad) = True Then
    Workbooks(Dateiname).Activate
    GoTo ende
    Else
    If MsgBox("Eine Englische Version existiert schon." & vbLf & vbLf & _
    "Datei jetzt Ãķffnen ?", vbYesNo + vbQuestion) = vbYes Then
    ActiveWorkbook.Save
    GoTo Weiter
    Else
    GoTo ende
End If
End If
End If

Application.EnableEvents = False

If ActiveSheet.Range("A2").Value = 1 Then
MsgBox ("Bitte die Datei erst Speichern"), vbInformation
GoTo ende
End If
'
'
'Call Zaehler
'ActiveWorkbook.Save
'ActiveSheet.Range("A2").Value = 0

' code to get find_str and repl_str
  With ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("1")
  ' put table in range array
    repl_arr = .Range("repl_table").Value
  End With

' make replacements for each non empty value in
' replacement table
  For i = 1 To UBound(repl_arr)
    If Not IsEmpty(repl_arr(i, 1)) Then
      ActiveSheet.Cells.Replace What:=repl_arr(i, 1), _
                                Replacement:=repl_arr(i, 2)
    End If
  Next i

Cells(1, 1).Value = "2"

Zeile = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value + 2

If Cells(1, 1).Value = "2" Then
    Rows(Zeile).Hidden = True
End If

ActiveWorkbook.SaveCopyAs Filename:=Pfad & Dateiname

' code to get find_str and repl_str
  With ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("1")
  ' put table in range array
    repl_arr = .Range("repl_table").Value
  End With

' make replacements for each non empty value in
' replacement table
  For i = 1 To UBound(repl_arr)
    If Not IsEmpty(repl_arr(i, 2)) Then
      ActiveSheet.Cells.Replace What:=repl_arr(i, 2), _
                                Replacement:=repl_arr(i, 1)
    End If
  Next i

Cells(1, 1).Value = "1"

If Cells(1, 1).Value = "1" Then
    Rows(Zeile).Hidden = False
End If


If ActiveSheet.Range("AL7").Value = "UF_open" Then
Call UserForm3.OpenFiles 'Modul 13
End If

Weiter:

ActiveSheet.Range("A2").Value = 0

ActiveSheet.Range("AK1").Value = ActiveWorkbook.FullName

On Error Resume Next

ende:

Sub Englisch_Deutsch()
Dim find_str As String, repl_str As String
Dim repl_arr As Variant
Dim i As Variant
Dim Pfad As String
Dim Dateiname As String
Dim sPfad As String

Dim Zeile As Integer

Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Application.EnableEvents = False

On Error Resume Next

Range("S3").Select

Call Netzwerkstatus

If ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "NEIN" Then
GoTo ende
End If

If ActiveSheet.Range("A1").Value = 1 Then
GoTo ende
End If

Dateiname = "RAP_" & Range("S3") & ".xlsm"

Pfad = ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value

If Dir(Pfad & Dateiname) <> "" Then
    sPfad = Pfad & Dateiname
    If DateiGeoeffnet(sPfad) = True Then
    Workbooks(Dateiname).Activate
    GoTo ende
    Else
        If ActiveSheet.Range("A2").Value = 1 Then
        ActiveWorkbook.Save
        Workbooks.Open Filename:=Pfad & Dateiname
        Else
        Workbooks.Open Filename:=Pfad & Dateiname
        End If
    End If
Else
MsgBox ("Eine Deutsche Version ist nicht vorhanden!"), vbInformation
GoTo ende
End If

ende:

Option Explicit
Public schlieÃen As Boolean
Private mblnNoEvent As Boolean
Function Ping(strHost As String) As Boolean

Dim oPing, oRetStatus

Set oPing = GetObject("winmgmts:{impersonationLevel=impersonate}") _
    .ExecQuery("SELECT *" _
        & " FROM Win32_PingStatus" _
            & " WHERE address='" & strHost & "'")
For Each oRetStatus In oPing
Ping = Not (IsNull(oRetStatus.StatusCode) _
        Or oRetStatus.StatusCode <> 0)
Next oRetStatus

End Function

Sub Datei__speichern()

Dim Dateiname As String
Dim Projektpfad As String
Dim DesktopPfad As String
Dim Antwort As Integer

Dim FSO As Object
Dim unterordner As Object
Dim Ordner As Object
Dim quellordner As String
Dim suchname As String

Dim strIP As String

Dim sMldg As String
Dim sTitel As String
Dim iRes As Integer

Dim r

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

On Error Resume Next

r = ActiveCell.Address

If ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("S3").Value = "" Then 'angegebenes Blatt angegebener Bereich
Call beenden
MsgBox ("Die Datei kann ohne Auftrags-Nr. nicht gespeichert werden."), vbInformation
GoTo ende
End If

strIP = "10.150.6.12"
    
If Ping(strIP) Then
ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "JA"
Else
ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "NEIN"
GoTo Weiter
End If

Set FSO = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")

'quellordner = "\\mueller-file-01\Auftraege\" & ActiveSheet.Range("AK3").Value & "\"
quellordner = "U:\" & ActiveSheet.Range("AK3").Value & "\"
suchname = ActiveSheet.Range("AL3").Value

ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value = ""

Set unterordner = FSO.getfolder(quellordner).subfolders
For Each Ordner In unterordner
    If VBA.Left(Ordner.Name, Len(suchname)) = suchname Then _
   ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value = quellordner & Ordner.Name & "\" & "Rohbauabnahme" & "\" 'MsgBox ordner.Name
Next

Application.EnableEvents = False

Weiter:

Application.GoTo Reference:=Range("A1"), Scroll:=True
Range("S3").Select

If Cells(1, 1).Value = "1" Then
Dateiname = "RAP_" & Range("S3") & ".xlsm"
End If

If Cells(1, 1).Value = "2" Then
Dateiname = "RAP_" & Range("S3") & "_E" & ".xlsm"
End If

Projektpfad = ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value

If Not ActiveSheet.Range("AJ1").Value = ActiveSheet.Range("AK10").Value Then
    If ActiveSheet.Range("AL11").Value = "NeueDatei" And ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "JA" Then
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False
    Call Zaehler 'Modul 5
    Call Daten_auslesen ' Modul 9
    ActiveWorkbook.SaveAs Filename:=Projektpfad & Dateiname
    ActiveSheet.Range("AL11").Value = "KeineNeueDatei"
    Application.DisplayAlerts = True
    Else
        If ActiveSheet.Range("AL11").Value = "KeineNeueDatei" And ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "JA" Then
        If Dir(Projektpfad & Dateiname) <> "" Then
        Antwort = MsgBox("FÃžr diese Auftrags- Nr. ist bereits ein Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll vorhanden." _
        & vbLf & vbLf & "Soll dieses ersetzt werden?", vbYesNo + vbCritical, "Achtung!")
            If Antwort = vbNo Then
            GoTo ende
            Else
            If Antwort = vbYes Then
            Application.DisplayAlerts = False
            Call Zaehler 'Modul 5
            Call Daten_auslesen ' Modul 9
            ActiveWorkbook.SaveAs Filename:=Projektpfad & Dateiname
            ActiveSheet.Range("AL11").Value = "NeueDatei"
            Application.DisplayAlerts = True
            End If
            End If
        Else
        Application.DisplayAlerts = False
        Call Zaehler 'Modul 5
        Call Daten_auslesen ' Modul 9
        ActiveWorkbook.SaveAs Filename:=Projektpfad & Dateiname
        Application.DisplayAlerts = True
End If
End If
End If
End If

If ActiveSheet.Range("AJ1").Value = ActiveSheet.Range("AK10").Value Then
    If ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "JA" Then
    Call Zaehler 'Modul 5
    Call Daten_auslesen ' Modul 9
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False
    ActiveWorkbook.SaveAs Filename:=Projektpfad & Dateiname
    Application.DisplayAlerts = True
     
End If
End If

DesktopPfad = ActiveSheet.Range("AL10").Value

If ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "NEIN" Then
MsgBox ("... der Computer hat keine Verbindung mit dem Netzwerk.") & vbLf & vbLf & _
("Die Daten werden jetzt in einer Datei auf Desktop gespeichert!") & vbLf & vbLf & _
("Damit die Daten im Originaldokument gespeichert werden,") & vbLf & _
("bitte zu einem spÃĪteren Zeitpunkt die Netzwerverbindung herstellen und diese Datei erneut speichern."), vbInformation
Application.DisplayAlerts = False
Call Zaehler 'Modul 5
On Error Resume Next
ActiveWorkbook.SaveAs Filename:=DesktopPfad & Dateiname
Application.DisplayAlerts = True
End If

ActiveSheet.Range("A2").Value = 0
ActiveSheet.Range("AJ1").Value = ActiveWorkbook.Name
ActiveSheet.Range("AK1").Value = ActiveWorkbook.FullName
ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value = ActiveWorkbook.Path & "\"

Application.ScreenUpdating = False
If ActiveSheet.Range("AL7").Value = "UF_open" Then
Call UserForm3.OpenFiles 'Modul 13
End If
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

ende:

Application.EnableEvents = False

Range(r).Select

Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

Ergebnis2 = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(Bereich1, "<>")

End If

    .LeftFooter = "Auftrags -Nr.: " & "&""Arial,Fett ""&11 " & Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("S3") & "&""Arial,Standard ""&10 " & vbLf & _
                    "Aufbautyp: " & Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("F4") & " " & _
                    Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("I4") & vbLf & _
                    "Kunde: " & Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("F3")

    .RightFooter = "&""Arial,Fett ""&11 " & "Seite: &P von &N"
    
End With

With ActiveSheet
.PrintPreview
End With

ende:

End If

ActiveSheet.Range("AL7").Value = ""    ' Setzt die Bedingung wieder zurÃžck

Sub Speichern__pdf()

Dim Dateiname As String
Dim xlOpenAfterPublish As Boolean
Dim Projektpfad As String
Dim Antwort As Integer

Dim ZeileStart As Integer
Dim SpalteStart As Integer
Dim ZeileEnde As Integer
Dim SpalteEnde As Integer
Dim ZeileEnde1 As Long
Dim i As Long

Dim Bereich1 As Range
Dim Bereich2 As Range
Dim Zelle As Range

Call Netzwerkstatus 'Modul 12

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

If ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("S3").Value = "" Then 'angegebenes Blatt angegebener Bereich
MsgBox ("Die Datei kann ohne Auftrags-Nr. nicht gespeichert werden."), vbInformation
GoTo ende
End If

If ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "NEIN" Then
GoTo ende
End If

On Error Resume Next

Dateiname = "RAP_" & Range("S3") & ".pdf"

Projektpfad = ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value

If Dir(Projektpfad & Dateiname) <> "" Then
Antwort = MsgBox("FÃžr diesen Auftrag ist bereits eine Datei mit dem Namen " & Dateiname & " vorhanden." _
& vbLf & vbLf & "Soll dieses ersetzt werden?", vbYesNo + vbQuestion, "Info")
If Antwort = vbNo Then
GoTo ende
Else
If Antwort = vbYes Then
GoTo Weiter
End If
End If
End If
            
Weiter:

Worksheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Shapes("PDF_intern").Visible = True

''' Hier werden die Preise der Technische Ãnderungen ein oder ausgeblendet.
''' Button Preise

Worksheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Activate

ZeileStart = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A5").Value + 1
SpalteStart = 21

ZeileEnde = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1
SpalteEnde = 23

ZeileEnde1 = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1

Set Bereich1 = Range(Cells(ZeileStart, SpalteStart), Cells(ZeileEnde, SpalteEnde))
Set Bereich2 = Range(Cells(ZeileStart, 56), Cells(ZeileEnde, 58))
Set Zelle = Range(Cells(ZeileStart, 21), Cells(ZeileStart, 23))

Dim a%

a = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountA([Bereich1])
If a > 0 Then
        Bereich1.Select
        Selection.Copy
        Bereich2.Select
        Selection.PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks _
        :=False, Transpose:=False
        Application.CutCopyMode = False
        Bereich1.Select
        Selection.ClearContents
        Zelle.Select
    Else
        mblnNoEvent = False
End If

Range("Bereich_Unterschrift").EntireRow.Hidden = True

Dateiname = "RAP_" & Range("S3") & ".pdf"

Projektpfad = ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value

Call Zaehler 'Modul 5

ActiveSheet.ExportAsFixedFormat Type:=xlTypePDF, Filename:=Projektpfad & Dateiname _
 , Quality:=xlQualityStandard, IncludeDocProperties:=True, IgnorePrintAreas:=False, OpenAfterPublish:=False

Bereich2.Select
Selection.Copy
Bereich1.Select
Selection.PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteValues, Operation:=xlNone, SkipBlanks _
:=False, Transpose:=False
Application.CutCopyMode = False
Bereich2.Select
Selection.ClearContents
Zelle.Select

Application.ScreenUpdating = False
If ActiveSheet.Range("AL7").Value = "UF_open" Then
Call UserForm3.OpenFiles 'Modul 13
End If

ende:

Worksheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Shapes("PDF_intern").Visible = False

Range("Bereich_Unterschrift").EntireRow.Hidden = False

Application.ScreenUpdating = False
If ActiveSheet.Range("AL7").Value = "UF_open" Then
Call UserForm3.OpenFiles 'Modul 13
End If

Range("F3").Select

Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

Sub LinkPDF__versenden()

Dim RAP As String
Dim auftrag  As String
Dim kunde  As String
Dim aufbau  As String

Dim olApp As Object
Dim oDummyText As String

Dim Dateiname As String
Dim Projektpfad As String


On Error Resume Next

If ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("S3").Value = "" Then 'angegebenes Blatt angegebener Bereich
MsgBox ("Keine.pdf Datei gefunden.") & vbLf & vbLf & ("Bitte erst eine Auftrags- Nr. vergeben und die Datei als .pdf speichern."), vbInformation
GoTo ende
End If

Call Netzwerkstatus 'Modul 12

If ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "NEIN" Then
GoTo ende
End If

Application.EnableEvents = False

Range("F3").Select

RAP = "RAP_"
auftrag = Range("S3")
kunde = Range("F3")
aufbau = Range("F4")

Dateiname = "RAP_" & Range("S3") & ".pdf"
Projektpfad = ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value

If Dir(Projektpfad & Dateiname) <> "" Then
GoTo Weiter
Else
MsgBox ("FÃžr diesen Auftrag ist noch kein .pdf Dokument erstellt worden.") _
        & vbLf & vbLf & ("Bitte erst als .pdf speichern."), vbCritical, "Achtung!"

GoTo ende
End If

Weiter:

Application.Cursor = xlWait

Set olApp = CreateObject("Outlook.Application")
With olApp.CreateItem(0)
.To = ""
.Subject = RAP & kunde & "_" & auftrag
.GetInspector.Display
oDummyText = .HTMLBody
.BodyFormat = 2
.HTMLBody = "Zur Info!<br><br>" & _
            "<br><br>" & "Kunde:" & VBA.Space(5) & kunde & "<br><br>" & "Aufbau:" & VBA.Space(5) & aufbau & "<br><br>" & "Bitte dem Link folgen:  " & VBA.Space(5) & _
            "<a href=""file://" & Projektpfad & Dateiname & """>" & _
                         RAP & auftrag & ".pdf" & .HTMLBody
End With

Application.Cursor = xlDefault

ende:

Range("F3").Select

Application.EnableEvents = True


End Sub

Sub LinkDatei__versenden()

Dim RAP As String
Dim auftrag  As String
Dim kunde  As String
Dim aufbau  As String

Dim olApp As Object
Dim oDummyText As String

Dim Dateiname As String


On Error Resume Next

If ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("S3").Value = "" Then 'angegebenes Blatt angegebener Bereich
MsgBox ("Die Datei kann als Link noch nicht versendet werden.") & vbLf & vbLf & ("Bitte die Datei erst speichern."), vbInformation
GoTo ende
End If

Call Netzwerkstatus 'Modul 12

If ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "NEIN" Then
GoTo ende
End If

Range("F3").Select

RAP = "RAP_"
auftrag = Range("S3")
kunde = Range("F3")
aufbau = Range("F4")

If Cells(1, 1).Value = "1" Then
Dateiname = "RAP_" & Range("S3") & ".xlsm"
End If

If Cells(1, 1).Value = "2" Then
Dateiname = "RAP_" & Range("S3") & "_E" & ".xlsm"
End If

Application.Cursor = xlWait

Set olApp = CreateObject("Outlook.Application")
With olApp.CreateItem(0)
.To = ""
.Subject = RAP & kunde & "_" & auftrag
.GetInspector.Display
oDummyText = .HTMLBody
.BodyFormat = 2
.HTMLBody = "Zur Info!<br><br>" & _
            "<br><br>" & "Kunde:" & VBA.Space(5) & kunde & "<br><br>" & "Aufbau:" & VBA.Space(5) & aufbau & "<br><br>" & "Bitte dem Link folgen:  " & VBA.Space(5) & _
            "<a href=""file://" & ActiveWorkbook.FullName & """>" & _
                         RAP & auftrag & ".xlsm" & .HTMLBody
End With

Application.Cursor = xlDefault

ende:

Range("F3").Select

End Sub

Sub Daten_auslesen()

Dim wksQuell As Worksheet
Dim wksZiel As Worksheet
Dim lngZeileQuell As Long
Dim lngZeileZiel As Long
Dim ersteZeileQuell As Long
Dim letzteZeileQuell As Long

On Error Resume Next

ActiveWorkbook.Worksheets("Fahrzeugbeleuchtung").Rows("2:100").Delete

Set wksQuell = ActiveWorkbook.Worksheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll")
Set wksZiel = ActiveWorkbook.Worksheets("Fahrzeugbeleuchtung")
lngZeileZiel = 2
ersteZeileQuell = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A3").Value + 1
letzteZeileQuell = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A4").Value - 1
For lngZeileQuell = ersteZeileQuell To letzteZeileQuell
 If Not wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 34).Text = "" Then
  wksZiel.Cells(lngZeileZiel, 1).Value = wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 34).Value
  wksZiel.Cells(lngZeileZiel, 2).Value = wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 35).Value
  wksZiel.Cells(lngZeileZiel, 3).Value = wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 36).Value
  wksZiel.Cells(lngZeileZiel, 4).Value = wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 37).Value
  wksZiel.Cells(lngZeileZiel, 5).Value = wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 38).Value
  wksZiel.Cells(lngZeileZiel, 6).Value = wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 39).Value
  lngZeileZiel = lngZeileZiel + 1
 End If
Next
Set wksQuell = Nothing
Set wksZiel = Nothing

On Error Resume Next

ActiveWorkbook.Worksheets("Techn. Ãnderung").Rows("2:100").Delete

Set wksQuell = ActiveWorkbook.Worksheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll")
Set wksZiel = ActiveWorkbook.Worksheets("Techn. Ãnderung")

letzteZeileQuell = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("A6").Value - 1
For lngZeileQuell = ersteZeileQuell To letzteZeileQuell
 If Not wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 32).Text = "" Then
  wksZiel.Cells(lngZeileZiel, 1).Value = wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 35).Value
  wksZiel.Cells(lngZeileZiel, 2).Value = wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 32).Value
  wksZiel.Cells(lngZeileZiel, 3).Value = wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 33).Value
  wksZiel.Cells(lngZeileZiel, 4).Value = wksQuell.Cells(lngZeileQuell, 34).Value

Option Explicit
Public Nureinmal As Boolean
Sub PrÃžfung_Kopfteil()
Dim chkRange As Range, myC As Range
Dim msg As String

On Error Resume Next

'In diesem Makro wird geprÃžft ob der Kopfteil (F3,F4,F9....) alle Zellen ausgefÃžllt sind
'Hier die Zellen eintragen die geprÃžft werden sollen
Set chkRange = Range("F3,F4,F9,F10,S3,S4")

'Ab hier nichts mehr ÃĪndern
msg = ""
For Each myC In chkRange
    If IsEmpty(myC) Then
        msg = msg & myC.Offset(0, -4).Text & vbCrLf
    End If
Next

Set chkRange = Nothing

If msg = "" Then
   Exit Sub
Else
    MsgBox "Folgende Zellen sind leer:" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & msg & vbCrLf & "Bitte ausfÃžllen!", vbInformation + vbOKOnly, "PrÃžfergebnis"
End If
End Sub

Sub PrÃžfung_Fahrzeugbeschriftung()
Dim chkRange As Range, myC As Range
Dim chkRange1 As Range, myC1 As Range
Dim msg As String
Dim msg1 As String

On Error Resume Next

'In diesem Makro wird geprÃžft ob alle Zellen in der Fahrzeugbeschriftung ausgefÃžllt sind
'Hier die Zellen eintragen die geprÃžft werden sollen
Set chkRange = Range("K30,K31,K32")
Set chkRange1 = Range("M33,M34,M35")

msg = ""
For Each myC In chkRange
    If IsEmpty(myC) Then
        msg = msg & myC.Offset(0, -9).Text & vbCrLf
    End If
Next
For Each myC1 In chkRange1
    If IsEmpty(myC1) Then
        msg1 = msg1 & myC1.Offset(0, -11).Text & vbCrLf
    End If
Next

Set chkRange = Nothing

If msg = "" And msg1 = "" Then
   Exit Sub
Else
    MsgBox "Folgende Zellen im Bereich Fahrzeugbeschriftung sind leer:" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & msg & msg1 & vbCrLf & "Bitte ausfÃžllen!", vbInformation + vbOKOnly, "PrÃžfergebnis"
End If
End Sub

Sub EinfÃĪrben()
Dim Zelle As Range, Bereich As Range, Wort As String

Wort = InputBox("Welches Wort rot fÃĪrben?", "Text fÃĪrben")
If Wort = "" Then Exit Sub
Set Bereich = ActiveCell
For Each Zelle In Bereich
If InStr(1, Zelle.Value, Wort) > 0 Then
With Zelle.Characters(Start:=InStr(1, Zelle.Value, Wort), _
Length:=Len(Wort)).Font
.ColorIndex = 3 ' rot
.Bold = True
End With
End If
Next Zelle
End Sub

VBA MACRO ufPicView.frm 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/ufPicView'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Option Explicit
Public ixPicNr As Integer

Private Declare PtrSafe Function FindWindow Lib "user32.dll" Alias "FindWindowA" ( _
    ByVal lpClassName As String, _
    ByVal lpWindowName As String) As Long
Private Declare PtrSafe Function GetWindowLong Lib "user32.dll" Alias "GetWindowLongA" ( _
    ByVal hwnd As Long, _
    ByVal nIndex As Long) As Long
Private Declare PtrSafe Function SetWindowLong Lib "user32.dll" Alias "SetWindowLongA" ( _
    ByVal hwnd As Long, _
    ByVal nIndex As Long, _
    ByVal dwNewLong As Long) As Long
Private Declare PtrSafe Function DrawMenuBar Lib "user32.dll" ( _
    ByVal hwnd As Long) As Long
Private Declare PtrSafe Function SendMessage Lib "user32.dll" Alias "SendMessageA" ( _
    ByVal hwnd As Long, _
    ByVal wMsg As Long, _
    ByVal wParam As Long, _
    ByRef lParam As Any) As Long
Private Declare PtrSafe Function ReleaseCapture Lib "user32.dll" () As Long

Private Const GC_CLASSNAMEMSEXCELFORM = "ThunderDFrame"
Private Const GWL_STYLE = -16
Private Const WS_CAPTION = &HC00000
Private Const HTCAPTION = 2
Private Const WM_NCLBUTTONDOWN = &HA1

Private hwndForm As Long

Private Sub cbExit_Click()
    ActiveSheet.Range("AI1").Value = 1
    Unload ufPicView
End Sub

Private Sub imgFrame_Click()
Unload ufPicView
ufPicView.Show vbModeless
'Call Start
End Sub

Private Sub UserForm_MouseDown(ByVal Button As Integer, _
    ByVal Shift As Integer, ByVal X As Single, ByVal Y As Single)
    If Button = 1 Then
        ReleaseCapture
        SendMessage hwndForm, WM_NCLBUTTONDOWN, HTCAPTION, 0&
    End If
End Sub
Private Sub cbBck_Click()
    If ixPicNr > 1 Then
        ixPicNr = ixPicNr - 1
        Call showPic
    End If
End Sub
Private Sub cbFwd_Click()
    ixPicNr = ixPicNr + 1
   Call showPic
End Sub

Private Sub UserForm_Activate()

Dim sngTop As Single, sngLeft As Single

On Error Resume Next

'''' Legt die Position der Userform fest.
''''

    StartUpPosition = 0
    
    With Application
    sngLeft = 460
    sngTop = 150

    Me.Left = sngLeft + Application.Left
    Me.Top = sngTop
    
    End With

hwndForm = FindWindow(GC_CLASSNAMEMSEXCELFORM, Me.Caption)

   If hwndForm <> 0 Then
        SetWindowLong hwndForm, GWL_STYLE, GetWindowLong(hwndForm, GWL_STYLE) And Not WS_CAPTION
        DrawMenuBar hwndForm
    End If
    
    If IsError(ActiveSheet.Cells(3 + ixPicNr, 35).Value) Then
        MsgBox "Es sind keine Bilder vorhanden"
        Me.Hide
    End If
    
    If ActiveSheet.Cells(1, 35).Value = 1 Then
    ixPicNr = 1
    Call showPic
    Else
    Call Start
    End If
End Sub
Private Sub showPic()
'''
''' Aktuell kÃķnnen max. 16 Bilder unter dem Dateipfad (C:\RAP_Bilder) eingefÃžgt werden.
'''
On Error Resume Next

    lblDir.Caption = ActiveSheet.Range("Verzeichnis").Value 'Breich Verzeichnis
    lblFile.Caption = ActiveSheet.Cells(3 + ixPicNr, 35).Value 'Ab Zeile 3 + 1 und Spalte 35
    imgFrame.Picture = LoadPicture(lblDir.Caption & "\" & lblFile.Caption)
    If IsError(ActiveSheet.Cells(4 + ixPicNr, 35).Value) Then cbFwd.Visible = False
    If Not IsError(ActiveSheet.Cells(4 + ixPicNr, 35).Value) Then cbFwd.Visible = True

    If ixPicNr = 1 Then
    cbBck.Visible = False
    Else
    cbBck.Visible = True
    End If

    ActiveSheet.Range("AI1").Value = ixPicNr
End Sub
Private Sub Start()
ixPicNr = ActiveSheet.Cells(1, 35).Value
Call showPic
End Sub

VBA MACRO Modul12.bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Modul12'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Option Explicit
Function Ping(strHost As String) As Boolean

Dim oPing, oRetStatus

Set oPing = GetObject("winmgmts:{impersonationLevel=impersonate}") _
    .ExecQuery("SELECT *" _
        & " FROM Win32_PingStatus" _
            & " WHERE address='" & strHost & "'")
For Each oRetStatus In oPing
Ping = Not (IsNull(oRetStatus.StatusCode) _
        Or oRetStatus.StatusCode <> 0)
Next oRetStatus

End Function

Sub Netzwerkstatus()

Dim strIP As String

Application.EnableEvents = False

strIP = "10.150.6.12"
 
If Ping(strIP) Then

ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "JA"

Else

ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "NEIN"
MsgBox ("... der Computer hat keine Verbindung mit dem Netzwerk.") & vbLf & vbLf & _
("Funktion nicht mÃķglich!"), vbInformation

End If

Application.EnableEvents = True

End Sub

Sub Netzwerkstatus_Fahrzeugbeschriftung()

Dim strIP As String

strIP = "10.150.6.12"
 
If Ping(strIP) Then

Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Cells(2, 36).Value = "U:\Bilder_RAP"
ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "JA"

Else

Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Cells(2, 36).Value = "C:\RAP_Bilder"
ActiveSheet.Range("A7").Value = "NEIN"

End If

End Sub

Public strPath As String
Option Explicit
Private t As Boolean

Private Declare PtrSafe Function ShellExecute Lib "shell32.dll" Alias "ShellExecuteA" _
(ByVal hwnd As Long, ByVal lpOperation As String, ByVal lpFile As String, _
ByVal lpParameters As String, ByVal lpDirectory As String, ByVal nShowCmd As Long) As Long
Public Sub Open_File(strFileName As String, windowType As Integer)
ShellExecute 0, "Open", strFileName, "", "", windowType
End Sub

'' Jede Mintue wird das Makro "generate_meldung" ausgefÃžhrt.
'' Das Makro "starten" wird gestartet wenn die Datei geÃķffnet wird.
'' Das Makro "beenden" wird beendet wenn die Datei geschlossen wird.

Sub starten()
Dim zeit As Date
t = True
zeit = Time + TimeSerial(0, 5, 0)
Application.OnTime zeit, "generate_meldung"
End Sub
Sub generate_meldung()
If ActiveSheet.Range("A10").Value = "" Then
Call Datei__speichern
End If
If t = True Then starten
End Sub
Sub beenden()
t = False
End Sub
Sub Auftrags_Ordner()

Application.EnableEvents = False

If UserForm3.Visible = True Then
Unload UserForm3
Else
    If ufPicView.Visible = True Or ufPicView_RBA.Visible = True Or _
    UserForm1.Visible = True Or UserForm2.Visible = True Then
    GoTo ende
    End If
    If Not ActiveSheet.Range("AM3").Value = "U:\" Then
    MsgBox ("Bitte die Datei erst im Netzwerk speichern.") & vbLf & vbLf & _
    ("Funktion nicht mÃķglich!"), vbInformation
    GoTo ende
    End If
    UserForm3.Show vbModeless
End If

ende:

Application.EnableEvents = True

End Sub

    Me.Top = sngTop
    
    End With

'        .WindowState = xlMaximized

   If hwndForm <> 0 Then

        DrawMenuBar hwndForm

Public Sub OpenFiles()
    Dim MyFile As String
    Dim Path As String
    
    ListBox1.Clear

    Set colFiles = New Collection
    Path = ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value
    MyFile = Dir$(Path & "*.*")
    Do Until MyFile = ""
        ListBox1.AddItem MyFile
        colFiles.Add Path & MyFile, MyFile
        MyFile = Dir
    Loop

Label2.Caption = Sheets("FB_Rohbauabnahmeprotokoll").Range("AL13").Value
'UserForm4.Label1.Caption = ""
'UserForm4.Label1.Caption = ActiveSheet.Range("AL13").Value

End Sub

VBA MACRO Modul14.bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Modul14'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Option Explicit

Sub AuftragsOrdner_finden()
Dim FSO As Object
Dim unterordner As Object
Dim Ordner As Object
Dim quellordner As String
Dim quellordnerUF As String
Dim suchname As String
Dim Dateiname As String

On Error Resume Next

Application.EnableEvents = False

Set FSO = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")

'quellordner = "\\mueller-file-01\Auftraege\" & ActiveSheet.Range("AK3").Value & "\"
quellordner = "U:\" & ActiveSheet.Range("AK3").Value & "\"
suchname = ActiveSheet.Range("AL3").Value

quellordnerUF = "U: \ " & ActiveSheet.Range("AK3").Value & " \ " 'Zeigt den OrdnerPfad in der UserForm an mit Leerzeichen " \ "

ActiveSheet.Range("AK4").Value = ""
ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value = ""

Set unterordner = FSO.getfolder(quellordner).subfolders
For Each Ordner In unterordner
    If VBA.Left(Ordner.Name, Len(suchname)) = suchname Then _
    ActiveSheet.Range("AK4").Value = Ordner.Name 'MsgBox ordner.Name
Next

Application.EnableEvents = False

If ActiveSheet.Range("AK4").Value = "" Then
    MsgBox ("Kein Auftragsordner gefunden!" & vbLf & vbLf & "Bitte Auftrags- Nr. prÃžfen."), vbInformation
    ActiveSheet.Range("F3").Value = ""
    ActiveSheet.Range("F4").Value = ""
    ActiveSheet.Range("S3").Value = ""
Else
    ActiveSheet.Range("F3").Value = ActiveSheet.Range("AK6")
    ActiveSheet.Range("F4").Value = ActiveSheet.Range("AK7")
    ActiveSheet.Range("AL1").Value = quellordner & ActiveSheet.Range("AK4") & "\" & "Rohbauabnahme" & "\"
    ActiveSheet.Range("AO2").Value = quellordner & ActiveSheet.Range("AK4") & "\" & "Fotos Rohbauabnahme"
    ActiveSheet.Range("AL13").Value = quellordnerUF & ActiveSheet.Range("AK4") & " \ " & "Rohbauabnahme" & " \"
End If

If ActiveSheet.Range("AK5").Value = "" And ActiveSheet.Range("AK4").Value <> "" Then
    MsgBox ("Kein Auftragsordner gefunden!" & vbLf & vbLf & "Bitte Auftrags-Nr. prÃžfen."), vbInformation
    ActiveSheet.Range("F3").Value = ""
    ActiveSheet.Range("F4").Value = ""
    ActiveSheet.Range("S3").Value = ""
End If

Application.ScreenUpdating = False
If ActiveSheet.Range("AL7").Value = "UF_open" Then
Call UserForm3.OpenFiles 'Modul 13
End If
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

Application.EnableEvents = True

End Sub

Sub RAP_prÃžfen()

Dim quelldatei As String

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False


quelldatei = ActiveSheet.Range("AL15").Value

If Dir(quelldatei) <> "" Then
ActiveSheet.Range("AL11").Value = "KeineNeueDatei"
End If

Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

Private Sub UserForm_MouseDown(ByVal Button As Integer, _
    ByVal Shift As Integer, ByVal X As Single, ByVal Y As Single)
    If Button = 1 Then
        ReleaseCapture
        SendMessage hwndForm, WM_NCLBUTTONDOWN, HTCAPTION, 0&
    End If
End Sub
Private Sub cbBck_Click()
    If ixPicNr > 1 Then
        ixPicNr = ixPicNr - 1
        Call showPic
    End If
End Sub
Private Sub cbFwd_Click()
    ixPicNr = ixPicNr + 1
   Call showPic
End Sub

Private Sub UserForm_Activate()

Dim sngTop As Single, sngLeft As Single

On Error Resume Next

'''' Legt die Position der Userform fest.
''''

     StartUpPosition = 0
    With Application
        .WindowState = xlMaximized
        Me.Top = Application.Top
        Me.Left = Application.Left
        Me.Height = Application.Height
        Me.Width = Application.Width
     End With
     
hwndForm = FindWindow(GC_CLASSNAMEMSEXCELFORM, Me.Caption)

   If hwndForm <> 0 Then
        SetWindowLong hwndForm, GWL_STYLE, GetWindowLong(hwndForm, GWL_STYLE) And Not WS_CAPTION
        DrawMenuBar hwndForm
    End If
    
    If IsError(ActiveSheet.Cells(121 + ixPicNr, 79).Value) Then
        MsgBox "Es sind keine Bilder vorhanden"
        Me.Hide
    End If
    
    If ActiveSheet.Cells(1, 40).Value = 1 Then
    ixPicNr = 1
    Call showPic
    Else
    Call Start_RBA
    End If
End Sub
Private Sub showPic()
'''
''' Aktuell kÃķnnen max. 16 Bilder unter dem Dateipfad (C:\RAP_Bilder) eingefÃžgt werden.
'''
On Error Resume Next

    lblDir.Caption = ActiveSheet.Range("Verzeichnis_Bilder_RBA").Value 'Breich Verzeichnis
    lblFile.Caption = ActiveSheet.Cells(121 + ixPicNr, 79).Value 'Ab Zeile 3 + 1 und Spalte 35
    imgFrame1.Picture = LoadPicture(lblDir.Caption & "\" & lblFile.Caption)
    If IsError(ActiveSheet.Cells(122 + ixPicNr, 79).Value) Then cbFwd.Visible = False
    If Not IsError(ActiveSheet.Cells(122 + ixPicNr, 79).Value) Then cbFwd.Visible = True

    If ixPicNr = 1 Then
    cbBck.Visible = False
    Else
    cbBck.Visible = True
    End If

    ActiveSheet.Range("AN1").Value = ixPicNr
End Sub
Private Sub Start_RBA()
ixPicNr = ActiveSheet.Cells(1, 35).Value
Call showPic
End Sub

+----------+--------------------+---------------------------------------------+
|Type      |Keyword             |Description                                  |
+----------+--------------------+---------------------------------------------+
|AutoExec  |Workbook_Open       |Runs when the Excel Workbook is opened       |
|AutoExec  |Workbook_BeforeClose|Runs when the Excel Workbook is closed       |
|AutoExec  |Aufbautyp_Click     |Runs when the file is opened and ActiveX     |
|          |                    |objects trigger events                       |
|AutoExec  |Worksheet_Change    |Runs when the file is opened and ActiveX     |
|          |                    |objects trigger events                       |
|Suspicious|Environ             |May read system environment variables        |
|Suspicious|Open                |May open a file                              |
|Suspicious|put                 |May write to a file (if combined with Open)  |
|Suspicious|Binary              |May read or write a binary file (if combined |
|          |                    |with Open)                                   |
|Suspicious|Kill                |May delete a file                            |
|Suspicious|Shell               |May run an executable file or a system       |
|          |                    |command                                      |
|Suspicious|vbNormalFocus       |May run an executable file or a system       |
|          |                    |command                                      |
|Suspicious|Run                 |May run an executable file or a system       |
|          |                    |command                                      |
|Suspicious|ShellExecute        |May run an executable file or a system       |
|          |                    |command                                      |
|Suspicious|ShellExecuteA       |May run an executable file or a system       |
|          |                    |command                                      |
|Suspicious|shell32             |May run an executable file or a system       |
|          |                    |command                                      |
|Suspicious|Call                |May call a DLL using Excel 4 Macros (XLM/XLF)|
|Suspicious|MkDir               |May create a directory                       |
|Suspicious|ActiveWorkbook.SaveA|May save the current workbook                |
|          |s                   |                                             |
|Suspicious|CreateObject        |May create an OLE object                     |
|Suspicious|GetObject           |May get an OLE object with a running instance|
|Suspicious|Windows             |May enumerate application windows (if        |
|          |                    |combined with Shell.Application object)      |
|Suspicious|FindWindow          |May enumerate application windows (if        |
|          |                    |combined with Shell.Application object)      |
|Suspicious|Lib                 |May run code from a DLL                      |
|Suspicious|SendKeys            |May control another application by simulating|
|          |                    |user keystrokes                              |
|Suspicious|Chr                 |May attempt to obfuscate specific strings    |
|          |                    |(use option --deobf to deobfuscate)          |
|Suspicious|Hex Strings         |Hex-encoded strings were detected, may be    |
|          |                    |used to obfuscate strings (option --decode to|
|          |                    |see all)                                     |
|Suspicious|Base64 Strings      |Base64-encoded strings were detected, may be |
|          |                    |used to obfuscate strings (option --decode to|
|          |                    |see all)                                     |
|IOC       |10.150.6.12         |IPv4 address                                 |
|IOC       |user32.dll          |Executable file name                         |
|IOC       |shell32.dll         |Executable file name                         |
|IOC       |explorer.exe        |Executable file name                         |
|Base64    |4B                  |NEIN                                         |
|String    |                    |                                             |
|Suspicious|VBA Stomping        |VBA Stomping was detected: the VBA source    |
|          |                    |code and P-code are different, this may have |
|          |                    |been used to hide malicious code             |
+----------+--------------------+---------------------------------------------+
VBA Stomping detection is experimental: please report any false positive/negative at https://github.com/decalage2/oletools/issues
